The idea is that since the user\n     * has yet to process the data for the partition that has already been fetched, we should not go send for more data\n     * until the previously-fetched data has been processed.\n     *\n     * @param buffered The set of partitions we have in our buffer\n     * @return {@link Set} of {@link TopicPartition topic partitions} for which we should fetch data\n     */\n    private Set<TopicPartition> fetchablePartitions(Set<TopicPartition> buffered) {\n        // This is the test that returns true if the partition is *not* buffered\n        Predicate<TopicPartition> isNotBuffered = tp -> !buffered.contains(tp);\n\n        // Return all partitions that are in an otherwise fetchable state *and* for which we don't already have some\n        // messages sitting in our buffer.\n        return new HashSet<>(subscriptions.fetchablePartitions(isNotBuffered));\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Determine from which replica to read: the <i>preferred</i> or the <i>leader</i>. records));\n        Map<TopicPartition, OffsetAndMetadata> nextOffsetAndMetadataMap = mkMap(mkEntry(partition, nextOffsetAndMetadata));\n        return new Fetch<>(recordsMap, positionAdvanced, records.size(), nextOffsetAndMetadataMap);\n    }\n\n    private Fetch(\n            Map<TopicPartition, List<ConsumerRecord<K, V>>> records,\n            boolean positionAdvanced,\n            int numRecords,\n            Map<TopicPartition, OffsetAndMetadata> nextOffsetAndMetadata\n    ) {\n        this.records = records;\n        this.positionAdvanced = positionAdvanced;\n        this.numRecords = numRecords;\n        this.nextOffsetAndMetadata = nextOffsetAndMetadata;\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Add another {@link Fetch} to this one; all of its records will be added to this fetch's\n     * {@link #records() records}, and if the other fetch\n     * {@link #positionAdvanced() advanced the consume position for any topic partition},\n     * this fetch will be marked as having advanced the consume position as well.\n     * @param fetch the other fetch to add; may not be null\n     */\n    public void add(Fetch<K, V> fetch) {\n        Objects.requireNonNull(fetch);\n        addRecords(fetch.records);\n        this.positionAdvanced |= fetch.positionAdvanced;\n        this.nextOffsetAndMetadata.putAll(fetch.nextOffsetAndMetadata);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * @return all of the non-control messages for this fetch, grouped by partition\n     */\n    public Map<TopicPartition, List<ConsumerRecord<K, V>>> records() {\n        return Collections.unmodifiableMap(records);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * @return whether the fetch caused the consumer's\n     * {@link org.apache.kafka.clients.consumer.KafkaConsumer#position(TopicPartition) position} to advance for at\n     * least one of the topic partitions in this fetch\n     */\n    public boolean positionAdvanced() {\n        return positionAdvanced;\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * offsets and metadata that the consumer will consume (last epoch is included)\n     */\n    public Map<TopicPartition, OffsetAndMetadata> nextOffsets() {\n        return Map.copyOf(nextOffsetAndMetadata);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * @return {@code true} if and only if this fetch did not return any user-visible (i.e., non-control) records, and\n     * did not cause the consumer position to advance for any topic partitions\n     */\n    public boolean isEmpty() {\n        return numRecords == 0 && !positionAdvanced;\n    }\n\n    private void addRecords(Map<TopicPartition, List<ConsumerRecord<K, V>>> records) {\n        records.forEach((partition, partRecords) -> {\n            this.numRecords += partRecords.size();\n            List<ConsumerRecord<K, V>> currentRecords = this.records.get(partition);\n            if (currentRecords == null) {\n                this.records.put(partition, partRecords);\n            } else {\n                // this case shouldn't usually happen because we only send one fetch at a time per partition,\n                // but it might conceivably happen in some rare cases (such as partition leader changes).\n                // we have to copy to a new list because the old one may be immutable\n                List<ConsumerRecord<K, V>> newRecords = new ArrayList<>(currentRecords.size() + partRecords.size());\n                newRecords.addAll(currentRecords);\n                newRecords.addAll(partRecords);\n                this.records.put(partition, newRecords);\n            }\n There is at most one\n * {@link CompletedFetch} per partition in the queue.\n *\n * <p/>\n *\n * <em>Note</em>: this class is thread-safe with the intention that {@link CompletedFetch the data} will be\n * \"produced\" by a background thread and consumed by the application thread.\n */\npublic class FetchBuffer implements AutoCloseable {\n\n    private final Logger log;\n    private final ConcurrentLinkedQueue<CompletedFetch> completedFetches;\n    private final Lock lock;\n    private final Condition notEmptyCondition;\n    private final IdempotentCloser idempotentCloser = new IdempotentCloser();\n\n    private final AtomicBoolean wokenup = new AtomicBoolean(false);\n\n    private CompletedFetch nextInLineFetch;\n\n    public FetchBuffer(final LogContext logContext) {\n        this.log = logContext.logger(FetchBuffer.class);\n        this.completedFetches = new ConcurrentLinkedQueue<>();\n        this.lock = new ReentrantLock();\n        this.notEmptyCondition = lock.newCondition();\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Returns {@code true} if there are no completed fetches pending to return to the user.\n     *\n     * @return {@code true} if the buffer is empty, {@code false} otherwise\n     */\n    boolean isEmpty() {\n        try {\n            lock.lock();\n            return completedFetches.isEmpty();\n        } finally {\n            lock.unlock();\n        }\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Return whether we have any completed fetches pending return to the user. This method is thread-safe. The method will block, returning only\n     * under one of the following conditions:\n     *\n     * <ol>\n     *     <li>The buffer was already non-empty on entry</li>\n     *     <li>The buffer was populated during the wait</li>\n     *     <li>The remaining time on the {@link Timer timer} elapsed</li>\n     *     <li>The thread was interrupted</li>\n     * </ol>\n     *\n     * @param timer Timer that provides time to wait\n     */\n    void awaitNotEmpty(Timer timer) {\n        try {\n            lock.lock();\n\n            while (isEmpty() && !wokenup.compareAndSet(true, false)) {\n                // Update the timer before we head into the loop in case it took a while to get the lock.\n                timer.update();\n\n                if (timer.isExpired()) {\n                    // If the thread was interrupted before we start waiting, it still counts as\n                    // interrupted from the point of view of the KafkaConsumer.poll(Duration) contract.\n                    // We only need to check this when we are not going to wait because waiting\n                    // already checks whether the thread is interrupted.\n                    if (Thread.interrupted())\n                        throw new InterruptException(\"Interrupted waiting for results from fetching records\");\n\n                    break;\n                }\n\n                if (!notEmptyCondition.await(timer.remainingMs(), TimeUnit.MILLISECONDS)) {\n                    break;\n                }\n            }\n        } catch (InterruptedException e) {\n            throw new InterruptException(\"Interrupted waiting for results from fetching records\", e);\n        } finally {\n            lock.unlock();\n            timer.update();\n        }\n    }\n\n    void wakeup() {\n        wokenup.set(true);\n        try {\n            lock.lock();\n            notEmptyCondition.signalAll();\n        } finally {\n            lock.unlock();\n        }\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Updates the buffer to retain only the fetch data that corresponds to the given partitions. Any previously\n     * {@link CompletedFetch fetched data} is removed if its partition is not in the given set of partitions.\n     *\n     * @param partitions {@link Set} of {@link TopicPartition}s for which any buffered data should be kept\n     */\n    void retainAll(final Set<TopicPartition> partitions) {\n        try {\n            lock.lock();\n\n            completedFetches.removeIf(cf -> maybeDrain(partitions, cf));\n\n            if (maybeDrain(partitions, nextInLineFetch))\n                nextInLineFetch = null;\n        } finally {\n            lock.unlock();\n        }\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Drains (i.e. <em>removes</em>) the contents of the given {@link CompletedFetch} as its data should not\n     * be returned to the user.\n     */\n    private boolean maybeDrain(final Set<TopicPartition> partitions, final CompletedFetch completedFetch) {\n        if (completedFetch != null && !partitions.contains(completedFetch.partition)) {\n            log.debug(\"Removing {} from buffered fetch data as it is not in the set of partitions to retain ({})\", completedFetch.partition, partitions);\n            completedFetch.drain();\n            return true;\n        } else {\n            return false;\n        }\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Return the set of {@link TopicPartition partitions} for which we have data in the buffer.\n     *\n     * @return {@link TopicPartition Partition} set\n     */\n    Set<TopicPartition> bufferedPartitions() {\n        try {\n            lock.lock();\n\n            final Set<TopicPartition> partitions = new HashSet<>();\n\n            if (nextInLineFetch != null && !nextInLineFetch.isConsumed()) {\n                partitions.add(nextInLineFetch.partition);\n            }\n\n            completedFetches.forEach(cf -> partitions.add(cf.partition));\n            return partitions;\n        } finally {\n            lock.unlock();\n        }\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public void
